<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>(14)&nbsp;Employee Benefit Plans  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><I>Profit Sharing Plan  </I></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In January&nbsp;2004, the Company amended its 401(k) Retirement Plan to, among other things, increase the employer's matching contribution rate, reduce the
eligibility period, and to cause employees of TSA Stores to vest 100% in matching contribution in their account as of January&nbsp;1, 2004, qualified defined contribution profit sharing plan to
include a 401(k) plan feature for all eligible </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>F-26</FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=2,SEQ=73,EFW="2155658",CP="THE SPORTS AUTHORITY, INC.",DN="1",CHK=977928,FOLIO='F-26',FILE='DISK046:[05DEN9.05DEN1679]FJ1679A.;15',USER='MBRADT',CD='14-APR-2005;15:36' -->
<A NAME="page_fj1679_1_27"> </A>
<BR>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>employees.
On August&nbsp;4, 2003, the TSA Stores,&nbsp;Inc. 401(k) Savings and Profit Sharing Plan was merged into the Company's plan. On August&nbsp;1, 2001 the Oshman's Profit Sharing Plan
was merged into the Company's plan. Participants vest in the Company's contributions at a rate of 20% per year after the first year of service. The plan provides for discretionary contributions, if
any, by the Company in amounts determined annually by the Board of Directors. The Company matching contributions were $1,921,000 in fiscal 2004, $1,405,000 in fiscal 2003, and $522,000 in fiscal 2002. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>(15)&nbsp;Deferred Compensation Plan  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company has a nonqualified Deferred Compensation Plan (the "DCP") for certain members of management. Eligible employees may contribute a portion of base
salary or bonuses to the plan annually. The DCP provides for additional matching contributions by the Company, with limitations similar to the Company's 401(k) plan, as well as discretionary
contributions in an amount determined by the Company prior to the end of each plan year. The Company made no matching contributions to the DCP during fiscal 2004, 2003 or 2002. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>(16)&nbsp;Stock Compensation Plans  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><I>Long Term Incentive Compensation Plan  </I></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In August&nbsp;2003, the Company adopted a long term incentive compensation plan (the "Long Term Incentive Compensation Plan") following approval by the
shareholders which authorizes the issuance of various equity based awards of 2,500,000 shares of common stock. As of January&nbsp;29, 2005, 632,375 options and 411,000 restricted stock units have
been issued and remain outstanding under the Long
Term Incentive Compensation Plan. Stock options are granted with an exercise price equal to the fair value of the underlying stock at the date of grant. Stock options have a ten-year term
and vest 25% per year over four years from the date of grant. Certain grants of stock options to our board of directors vest over periods ranging from one to three years. Restricted stock, recorded at
the fair value of the stock at the grant date, is granted to certain employees of the Company and either cliff vests after five years from the grant date or vests 20% per year over five years from the
date of grant. The Company recorded approximately $2.5 and $15.4&nbsp;million of unamortized compensation as a reduction to stockholders' equity in fiscal 2004 and 2003, respectively, related to
grants of restricted stock. These amounts are being amortized to compensation expense on a straight-line basis over the vesting period. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><I>Management Equity Plan  </I></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company adopted a management equity plan (the "Management Equity Plan") which authorized the issuance of common stock plus grants of options to purchase
shares of authorized but unissued common stock up to 3,000,000 combined shares and options. As of January&nbsp;29, 2005, 147,600 purchased shares of common stock, 876,170 options, and 170,058 shares
of restricted stock have been issued and remain outstanding under the Management Equity Plan. Stock options are granted with an exercise price equal to the estimated fair value of the underlying stock
at the date of grant. All stock options have a ten-year term and vest 20% per year over five years from the date of grant. Restricted stock, recorded at the fair value of the stock at the
grant date, is granted to certain employees of the Company and either cliff vests after five years from the grant date or vests 20% per year over five years from the date of grant. The Company
recorded no unamortized compensation in fiscal 2004 and approximately $0.1 and $0.2&nbsp;million of unamortized compensation as a reduction to stockholders' equity in fiscal 2003 and 2002,
respectively, related to grants of restricted stock under this Management Equity Plan. These amounts are being amortized to compensation expense on a straight-line basis over the vesting
period. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>F-27</FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='page-break-before:always'></p>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><I>Substitute Company Options  </I></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In connection with the merger with TSA, options outstanding under TSA's 2000 Stock Option and Stock Award Plan, the Salaried Employees' Stock Option and Stock
Award Plan and the Director Stock Plan were assumed by the Company. These substitute options were modified to Company options utilizing the same conversion ratio of 0.37 to one as the common stock and
dividing the exercise price of the previous options by the conversion ratio. The holders of TSA substitute options vested fully on August&nbsp;4, 2003. All such persons had their original terms
during which holders can exercise those options. As of August&nbsp;4, 2003, 4,008,059 TSA options were exchanged for 1,482,982 Company substitute options. As of January&nbsp;29, 2005, 657,010
options remain outstanding under the TSA substitute options. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Effective
April&nbsp;7, 2005 the Company accelerated the vesting of 339,893 previously unvested stock options that had been granted under the Long Term Incentive Compensation Plan and
the Management Equity Plan. These options had exercise prices greater than $29.79 and became exercisable immediately as a result of the vesting acceleration. Because these options have exercise prices
above the current market price of the Company's stock and are not fully achieving their original objectives of incentive compensation and employee retention, the acceleration may have a positive
effect on employee morale and retention. Accelerating the vesting on stock options that have exercise prices in excess of current market prices will reduce the Company's compensation expense in future
periods and not result in a charge in the current period. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>(17)&nbsp;Related Party Transactions  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Prior to the merger, Green Equity Investors, whose general partner is Leonard Green&nbsp;&amp; Associates, LP ("LGA"), owned approximately 26% of the outstanding
common stock of the Company, which equated to approximately 13% of the combined company post merger. In December&nbsp;2003, LGA sold 1.1&nbsp;million shares of stock, reducing its beneficial
interest in the Company to approximately 8%. In December&nbsp;2004, LGA distributed their remaining shares of stock to their partners. Thus, at January&nbsp;29, 2005, LGA owns no shares of Company
stock. The Company had a management services agreement with LGA whereby LGA received an annual retainer fee of $0.5&nbsp;million plus reasonable expenses for providing certain management, consulting
and financial planning services. The management services agreement also provided that LGA may receive reasonable and customary fees and reasonable expenses from time to time for providing financial
advisory and investment banking services in connection with major financial transactions that are undertaken. The management services agreement was due to terminate in January&nbsp;2004. In
September&nbsp;2003, the Company bought out the remaining term of the agreement for $0.2&nbsp;million. In addition, in the third quarter of 2003, the Company paid LGA a fee of
$4.25&nbsp;million, plus out-of-pocket expenses, in connection with the TSA merger which is included in the total purchase price paid. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
Company entered into a severance and noncancelable consulting agreement with Martin E. Hanaka, former Chairman of the Board and the former Chairman and CEO of TSA. Pursuant to the
severance agreement, Mr.&nbsp;Hanaka's employment with the Company ceased as of December&nbsp;31, 2003. Under this agreement, the Company will continue, until August&nbsp;3, 2006, to nominate
Mr.&nbsp;Hanaka, and, if elected by our shareholders, he shall serve as a Director. Pursuant to the terms of the agreement, Mr.&nbsp;Hanaka was paid a cash payment of $2.5&nbsp;million, was
awarded $1.0&nbsp;million in Company common stock, and his unvested equity awards became fully vested and remain exercisable until at least August&nbsp;4, 2006. The amounts related to this
agreement were recorded as merger integration costs in the accompanying Statement of Income. In addition and simultaneous with this agreement, the Company executed a consulting agreement with
Mr.&nbsp;Hanaka. Mr.&nbsp;Hanaka has agreed to provide consulting services to the Company focussing on the cultural integration and the long-term strategic growth of the Company and
the enhancement of the public reputation and image of the Company. Pursuant to the consulting agreement, the Company agreed to pay a fee of $100,000 per year to Mr.&nbsp;Hanaka and to pay his
related office expenses in Fort Lauderdale, Florida, for his services to be rendered over a period of approximately 31&nbsp;months, terminating August&nbsp;3, 2006. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>F-29</FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>(18)&nbsp;Contingencies  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><I>Legal Proceedings  </I></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company is, from time to time, involved in various legal proceedings and claims arising in the ordinary course of business. Management believes that the
outcome of all such pending legal proceedings to which the Company is a party will not, in the aggregate, have a material adverse effect on the Company's business, financial condition, operating
results, or cash flows. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;TSA
Stores is one of thirty-three named defendants, including firearms manufacturers, distributors and retailers, in City of Chicago and County of Cook v. Beretta U.S.A. Corp. et al.,
Circuit Court of Cook County, Illinois. This suit was served on TSA Stores in November&nbsp;1998. The original complaint was based on legal theories of public nuisance and negligent entrustment of
firearms and alleged that the defendants created a public nuisance by distributing, marketing and selling firearms in the portion of Cook County outside Chicago knowing or recklessly disregarding that
these guns would be illegally transferred and used in Chicago to commit crimes. The complaint sought damages allocated among the defendants exceeding $433&nbsp;million to compensate the City of
Chicago and Cook County for their alleged costs resulting from the alleged public nuisance. The complaint also sought punitive damages and injunctive relief imposing additional regulations on the
methods the defendants use to distribute, market and sell firearms in Cook County. In February&nbsp;2000, the Court dismissed the complaint's negligent entrustment count. The plaintiffs filed an
amended complaint with the Court's permission in March&nbsp;2000, which contained both the public nuisance and negligent entrustment counts. In September&nbsp;2000, the Court granted the motions
of the defendants to dismiss the amended complaint, in its entirety, with prejudice. In October&nbsp;2000, the plaintiffs appealed the dismissal of their public nuisance claim to the Appellate Court
of Illinois, First Judicial District. On November&nbsp;4, 2002, the Appellate Court reversed the dismissal of the public nuisance claim and remanded the case to the trial court for further
proceedings. While the other defendants filed a petition for leave to appeal before the Illinois Supreme Court, TSA Stores filed a petition for rehearing with the Appellate Court on
November&nbsp;25, 2002. The Appellate Court denied this motion on March&nbsp;7, 2003. On March&nbsp;27, 2003, TSA Stores filed an additional petition, as the other defendants had done
previously, for leave to appeal to the Illinois Supreme Court. On May&nbsp;5, 2003, the Illinois Supreme Court granted the plaintiffs' subsequent motion to hold the TSA Stores's petition in
abeyance, pending resolution of the other defendants' appeal. On September&nbsp;10, 2003, the Illinois Supreme Court heard oral arguments on the other defendants' appeal, and on November&nbsp;18,
2004, issued an opinion reversing the Appellate Court's decision and affirming the trial court's dismissal of the case. On January&nbsp;24, 2005, the Illinois Supreme Court denied the plaintiffs'
petition for rehearing. On January&nbsp;26, 2005, the Illinois Supreme Court exercised its supervisory authority to reverse the Appellate Court and affirmed the judgment of the trial court. The time
period for the plaintiffs to file&nbsp;a petition for a writ of certiorari to the United States Supreme Court has not run so we are currently unable to predict the outcome of this case. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>F-30</FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>(20)&nbsp;E-Commerce Agreement  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In June&nbsp;2001 and July&nbsp;2001, the former Gart Sports Company and former Sports Authority,&nbsp;Inc., respectively, entered into separate license and
e-commerce agreements with GSI, which expire on December&nbsp;31, 2011 and November&nbsp;8, 2019, respectively. Under the terms of the agreements, GSI developed and is currently
operating four online sporting goods stores at www.thesportsauthority.com, www.gartsports.com, www.sportmart.com, and www.oshmans.com. Under
these agreements, GSI owns certain content and technology related to the websites, purchases and owns the merchandise sold on the websites, and hosts, maintains, fulfills orders and furnishes all
other "back-end" operations required to operate the websites. GSI receives all revenue generated from the websites and pays the Company a royalty based on a certain percent of sales from
these sites. In connection with the e-commerce agreements, GSI granted Gart Sports a warrant to purchase 60,000 shares of common stock of GSI. A similar warrant for 30,000 GSI shares was
acquired from Oshman's at the time of the acquisition. The Company sold 60,000 of these warrants in October&nbsp;2001, and recognized a gain of $195,000. The remaining warrant to purchase 30,000
shares was exercised on November&nbsp;2, 2001, and the shares that were acquired upon exercise of the warrant were classified as available-for-sale marketable equity
securities and were sold in September&nbsp;2003 for a realized gain of $100,000. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2><B>(21)&nbsp;Stock Offering  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On May&nbsp;29, 2002, the Company completed a stock offering for 3.5&nbsp;million shares of common stock. This offering resulted in net proceeds of
approximately $52&nbsp;million from the sale of 1.75&nbsp;million new shares by the Company. The Company used the net proceeds to repay certain borrowings under the revolving line of credit
agreement with CIT Group/Business Credit,&nbsp;Inc. The balance of the shares was sold by selling stockholders, including Green Equity Investors, L.P. The Company did not receive any proceeds from
the sale of shares by selling stockholders. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><A

<A NAME="toc_ga1680_1"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>AMENDMENT NUMBER ONE<BR>  TO<BR>  FIRST AMENDED AND RESTATED FINANCING AGREEMENT    <BR>    </B></FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This AMENDMENT NUMBER ONE TO FIRST AMENDED AND RESTATED FINANCING AGREEMENT (this "Amendment"), dated as of April&nbsp;11, 2005, amends that certain First
Amended and Restated Financing Agreement, dated as of September&nbsp;15, 2004 (as may be amended from time to time, the "Financing Agreement"), executed by The Sports Authority,&nbsp;Inc., a
Delaware corporation ("Parent"), and each of the subsidiaries of Parent identified on the signature pages&nbsp;thereto ("Subsidiaries," together with the Parent shall be referred to herein as the
"Borrowers"), and The CIT Group/Business Credit,&nbsp;Inc., a New York corporation ("Agent"), for its benefit and the benefit of the lenders (such lenders are collectively referred to herein as the
"Lender Group") that are parties from time to time to the Financing Agreement. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><B>RECITALS  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, Agent, for its benefit and the benefit of the Lender Group, and Borrowers wish to amend the Financing Agreement pursuant to the terms and provisions set
forth in this Amendment as herein provided; and </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;NOW,
THEREFORE, the parties hereto agree as follows: </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><B>AGREEMENT  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Definitions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> Capitalized terms used herein and not otherwise defined herein, shall have the respective meanings set forth
in the Financing Agreement. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Applicable Margin Definition Amendment.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> The definition of "Applicable Margin" in the Financing Agreement is deleted and
the following substituted in place thereof: </FONT></P>

<UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><B>Applicable Margin</B></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" shall mean from and including the date of this Amendment, the Applicable Margin as may be increased or decreased, to
the relevant Applicable Margin set forth in the table below that corresponds to the highest pricing level (with level 4 being the lowest) with respect to which the Borrowers have met the Funded Debt
Ratio level set forth therein: </FONT></P>
</UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>Any
adjustment to the prevailing Applicable Margin shall be effective on the first (1st) Business Day of the month immediately following the date on which the Agent has received and reviewed Fiscal
Quarter end financial statements in accordance with any requirements established by the Agent for the preparation and delivery thereof. Notwithstanding anything in this Agreement to the contrary, in
the event that, the audited financial statements of the Borrowers required hereunder for such Fiscal Year shall indicate that the actual Funded Debt Ratio was higher for any Fiscal Quarter in such
Fiscal Year than previously reported in the quarterly financial statements for such quarter, then the Applicable Margin shall be adjusted retroactively (to the effective date of the Applicable Margin
which was based </FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=1,SEQ=1,EFW="2155658",CP="THE SPORTS AUTHORITY, INC.",DN="2",CHK=235124,FOLIO='blank',FILE='DISK047:[05DEN0.05DEN1680]GA1680A.;7',USER='MBRADT',CD='14-APR-2005;14:21' -->
<A NAME="page_ga1680_1_2"> </A>
<BR>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>upon
the delivery of such incorrect financial statements) to reflect the correct margin, and the Borrowers shall make payments to the Agent, for the ratable benefit of the Lenders, to reflect such
adjustment." </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Early Termination Fee Definition Amendment.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> The definition of "Early Termination Fee" in the Financing Agreement is
deleted and the following is substituted in place thereof: </FONT></P>

<UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><B>Early Termination Fee</B></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" shall: (a)&nbsp;mean the fee the Agent on behalf of the Lenders is entitled to charge the Borrowers (if any) in
the event the Borrowers or any one of them terminates the Line of Credit or this Financing Agreement on a date on or before August&nbsp;4, 2007; and (b)&nbsp;be determined by multiplying the Line
of Credit by (x)&nbsp;one half percent (0.5%) if the Early Termination Date occurs on or before August&nbsp;4, 2005, and (y)&nbsp;one quarter percent (0.25%) if the Early Termination Date occurs
after August&nbsp;4, 2005 but on or before August&nbsp;4, 2007. </FONT></P>

</UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Fixed Charge Coverage Ratio Definition Amendment.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> The definition of "Fixed Charge Coverage Ratio" in the Financing
Agreement is deleted and the following substituted in place thereof: </FONT></P>

<UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><B>Fixed Charge Coverage Ratio</B></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" shall mean, for the twelve (12)&nbsp;Fiscal Month period then ending, the ratio determined by dividing
EBITDA, less capital expenditures (as defined in accordance with GAAP; </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>provided, however</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>, solely for the purpose of this definition, in calculating
EBITDA and capital expenditures, tenant improvement allowances shall be treated as they have been historically treated by the Borrower prior to the Securities and Exchange Commission letter date
February&nbsp;7, 2005 clarifying lease accounting issues, without regard to GAAP) actually paid, by the sum of (a)&nbsp;all Interest Expense actually paid during such period, (b)&nbsp;principal
amounts paid on any Indebtedness other than the Obligations, and (c)&nbsp;all federal, state and local income tax expenses paid. </FONT></P>

</UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Amendment.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> The following definitions are added to the Financing Agreement: </FONT></P>

<UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><B>Funded Debt Ratio</B></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" shall mean the ratio determined by dividing TFFQ Average Debt by TFFQ EBITDA. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><B>TFFQ Average Debt</B></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" shall mean the average of all funded debt (including capital leases but excluding the construction loan for Paramus,
New Jersey in an amount up to Six Million Dollar ($6,000,000)) outstanding at the end of each fiscal quarter calculated by dividing the sum of the Funded Debt outstanding at the end of each of the
previous twelve (12)&nbsp;months, as shown on the financial statements prepared by the Borrower, by twelve (12). </FONT></P>

</UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Maturity Date Definition Amendment.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> The date of August&nbsp;4, 2008 in subsection&nbsp;(i)&nbsp;of the definition of
"Maturity Date" in the Financing Agreement is hereby deleted and the date of August&nbsp;4, 2009 is substituted in its place. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;11 Amendment.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> The date of August&nbsp;4, 2008 in Section&nbsp;11 of the Financing Agreement is hereby
deleted and the date August&nbsp;4, 2009 substituted in its place. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;14.12 Amendment.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> The date of August&nbsp;4, 2008 in the fourth line of Section&nbsp;14.12 of the
Financing Agreement is hereby deleted and the date of August&nbsp;4, 2009 is substituted in its place. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;C</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>ondition Precedent.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> The effectiveness of this Amendment is expressly conditioned upon the receipt by Agent of an executed
copy of this Amendment executed by Borrowers and each of the members of the Lender Group. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;10.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Entire Agreement.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> The Financing Agreement, as amended hereby, embodies the entire agreement and understanding between the
parties hereto and supersedes all prior agreements and understandings relating to the subject matter hereof. </FONT></P>

effect. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="RIGHT"><FONT SIZE=2><B>Exhibit 10.8  </B></FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="km1680_the_sports_authority,_inc._deferred_compensation_plan"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_km1680_1"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>THE SPORTS AUTHORITY,&nbsp;INC.<BR>  <BR>    DEFERRED COMPENSATION PLAN    <BR>    </B></FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;THE SPORTS AUTHORITY,&nbsp;INC., incorporated under the laws of the State of Delaware, (hereinafter referred to as the "Company"), hereby adopts the Gart Sports
Company Deferred Compensation Plan and restates the Plan as The Sports Authority,&nbsp;Inc. Deferred Compensation Plan (the "Plan"), effective as of January l, 2004. The Company intends to provide,
under the Plan, certain of its Key Employees with benefits, for the purpose of promoting in its Key Employees the strongest interest in the successful operation of the Company and to induce such
employees to remain in the employ of the Company. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE&nbsp;I<BR>
DEFINITIONS  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.01&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Beneficiary</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean any person, persons or entities designated by a Participant to receive benefits hereunder upon
the death of such Participant. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.02&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Benefit Account</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean the account maintained on the books of the Company for each Participant pursuant to
Section&nbsp;6.01 hereof, as adjusted daily for applicable earnings and losses, if any. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.03&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Bonus Contributions</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean deferral of bonus Compensation by Participant as provided in Article&nbsp;III of the
Plan. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.04&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Change of Control</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean the acquisition of beneficial ownership, after the Effective Date, directly or indirectly,
of more than fifty percent (50%) of the voting power of the outstanding common stock of the Company, by any person, group, association, corporation or other entity. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.05&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Code</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.06&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Company</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean The Sports Authority,&nbsp;Inc., a Delaware corporation, and its Subsidiaries and Affiliates, if
any. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.07&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Compensation</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean a Participant's income from the Company that is reported as wages on the Participant's
Form&nbsp;W-2 for income tax purposes for the year. Compensation shall include amounts that are not currently includable in the Employee's gross income by reason of the application of
Code Section&nbsp;402(e)(3), but shall not include any severance payments of any kind. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.08&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Deferral Change Date</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean, for purposes of changing the amount of Deferral Contributions under the Plan,
January&nbsp;1 of each Plan Year. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.09&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Deferral Contribution</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean deferral of Compensation by a Participant as provided in Article&nbsp;III of the
Plan. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.10&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Deferral Period</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean the period of time during which Compensation is being deferred pursuant to Article&nbsp;III
of the Plan. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.11&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Determination Date</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean the last day of the Plan Year. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.12&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Disability</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean total disability as determined by the insurance carrier under the Company's long term disability
plan. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.13&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Disallowed 401(k) Contributions</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean deferral of Compensation by a Participant as provided in Article&nbsp;III
of the Plan. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.14&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Early Retirement Age</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean the later of age 50 or five years of service. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.15&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Effective Date</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> of this Plan shall be January&nbsp;1, 1999; the effective date of the restatement of this Plan shall be
January&nbsp;1, 2004. </FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=1,SEQ=1,EFW="2155658",CP="THE SPORTS AUTHORITY, INC.",DN="3",CHK=172199,FOLIO='blank',FILE='DISK047:[05DEN0.05DEN1680]KM1680A.;8',USER='MBRADT',CD='14-APR-2005;15:32' -->
<A NAME="page_km1680_1_2"> </A>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.16&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Fiduciary Committee</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean the committee appointed pursuant to Article&nbsp;VIII of the Plan. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.17&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Hardship</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean an unforeseen financial emergency suffered by a Participant. The financial emergency must be beyond
the Participant's control and must be of sufficient magnitude to cause the Participant great hardship if early withdrawal of Participant's benefits were not allowed or if a change in Participant's
deferral elections were not allowed. Any early withdrawal by reason of Hardship shall be subject to the approval of the Fiduciary Committee and limited to the amount necessary to meet the financial
emergency, plus any applicable taxes based upon the applicable tax rate determined by the Company. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.18&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Involuntary Termination</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean Termination of Employment initiated by the Company, with or without cause. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.19&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Key Employees</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean all employees of the Company who are performing services for the Company, who are designated as
Key Employees by the Fiduciary Committee. A person designated as a Key Employee shall remain so until such designation is revoked by the Fiduciary Committee, in its sole discretion. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.20&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Normal Retirement Age</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean age 65. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.21&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Normal Retirement Date</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean the first day of the month after a Participant attains Normal Retirement Age and
actually retires. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.22&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Participant</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean a Key Employee of the Company who has completed election forms required and accepted by the
Fiduciary Committee as evidenced by an authorized signature. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.23&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Plan Entry Date</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean the first day of each calendar month after a Key Employee becomes eligible to participate in
the Plan, and after the Key Employee has a reasonable period of time to complete and file forms required by the Fiduciary Committee. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.24&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Plan Year</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean the twelve-month period on which the plan records are kept, which shall begin on January&nbsp;1
and end on December&nbsp;31 of each Plan Year. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.25&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;401(k) Plan</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean the qualified Section&nbsp;401(k) Profit-Sharing Plan maintained by the Company
which is qualified under Section&nbsp;401(a) of the Code. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.26&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Subsidiaries and Affiliates</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean any corporation or other employer during any period while it is, together with
the Company, a member of a controlled group of corporations or an affiliated service group under common control (within the meaning of Section&nbsp;414(b), (c)&nbsp;or (m)&nbsp;of the Code). </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.27&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Successor Company</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean any company which adopts this Plan for any former employees of Company who become employees
of a Successor Company under a plan of reorganization. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.28&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Termination of Employment</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> shall mean the Participant's ceasing to be employed by the Company for any reason whatsoever,
voluntary or involuntary, including by reason of death or Disability. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE&nbsp;II<BR>
ELIGIBILITY AND PARTICIPATION  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.01</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Participation.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;From time to time the Fiduciary Committee, in its sole discretion, may designate those Key
Employees to whom the opportunity to participate in this Plan shall be extended. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>2</FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=2,SEQ=2,EFW="2155658",CP="THE SPORTS AUTHORITY, INC.",DN="3",CHK=284851,FOLIO='2',FILE='DISK047:[05DEN0.05DEN1680]KM1680A.;8',USER='MBRADT',CD='14-APR-2005;15:32' -->
<A NAME="page_km1680_1_3"> </A>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.02</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Enrollment Requirements.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Key Employees who have been selected by the Fiduciary Committee to participate in
this Plan may enroll in the plan by completing such forms and furnishing such information as the Company may reasonably require. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.03</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Enrollment Time Period.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Key Employee must execute and submit forms the Company may reasonably require
no later than the day prior to the Plan Entry Date of the Plan Year in which the Key Employee has met the enrollment requirements. If the Key Employee does not enroll in the Plan as of the first Plan
Entry Date after which the Key Employee has met the enrollment requirements, the Key Employee will not be allowed to enroll in the Plan until the next Deferral Change Date. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.04</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Termination of Participation.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A Participant shall cease to be a Participant upon distribution of his vested
Account Balance, upon revocation by the Fiduciary Committee of the Participant's status as a Key Employee, or upon no longer meeting the definition of a management or highly compensated employee, as
these terms are used in Labor Regulation Section&nbsp;2520.104-23. A person who ceases to be a Participant during the Deferral Period will have no further right to subsequent
contributions under the Plan. However, the employment of a Participant shall not be deemed to be terminated by reason of an approved leave of absence granted in accordance with uniform rules applied
in a non-discriminatory manner by the Company. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.05</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Modification of Election.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A Participant may modify his or her form, timing and term of the benefit by
completing such forms and providing information as the Company may reasonably require at each Deferral Change Date. Any modification received by the Fiduciary Committee will supersede any prior
elections. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE&nbsp;III<BR>
PARTICIPANT CONTRIBUTIONS  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3.01</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Disallowed 401(k) Contributions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;For each Plan Year, if the Participant attempts to defer the maximum
amount permitted under the Section&nbsp;401(k) Plan, the Participant may elect to defer a portion of his or her Compensation which is equal to the amount distributed to the Participant during the
Plan Year from the Company's Section&nbsp;401(k) Plan as an excess deferral, excess contribution and/or excess aggregate contribution (as such terms are defined in the Company's
Section&nbsp;401(k) Plan), as adjusted for applicable earnings and losses, if any. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3.02</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Deferral Contributions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Participant may elect to make a Deferral Contribution of a portion of his or
her Compensation before the commencement of the pay period in which the election becomes effective. Deferral Contributions may not exceed fifty percent (50%) of Compensation, excluding bonus
Compensation. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3.03</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Bonus Contributions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Participant may elect to make a Bonus Contribution of a portion of his or her
bonus earned and payable on or after the Effective Date of this Plan. A Participant may elect to defer up to one hundred percent (100%) of any bonus payable to him, minus any applicable withholding. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3.04</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Subsequent Deferral and Bonus Contributions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Subsequent to the initial deferrals provided for in Sections
3.02 and 3.03 above, a Participant may from time to time elect to increase or decrease the amount of Compensation or bonus deferred in pay periods which commence on or after the next Deferral Change
Date which follows such subsequent election. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3.05</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Procedure for Deferral.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The initial election provided for in Sections 3.02 and 3.03 and any subsequent
election or elections provided for in Section&nbsp;3.04 shall be made on the forms provided by the Fiduciary Committee for that purpose. The amount specified in the election shall be deferred and </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>3</FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=3,SEQ=3,EFW="2155658",CP="THE SPORTS AUTHORITY, INC.",DN="3",CHK=99522,FOLIO='3',FILE='DISK047:[05DEN0.05DEN1680]KM1680A.;8',USER='MBRADT',CD='14-APR-2005;15:32' -->
<A NAME="page_km1680_1_4"> </A>
<BR>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>shall
be subtracted from the Compensation and bonus otherwise payable to the Participant during the period in which the election is in effect. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3.06</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Election to Defer Irrevocable; Exceptions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as otherwise provided herein, a Participant's election to
defer compensation shall be irrevocable except for changes allowed at each Deferral Change Date. The Fiduciary Committee, in its sole discretion, upon demonstration of a substantial Hardship by the
Participant, may permit subsequent alteration on a date other than such Deferral Change Date of a Participant's deferral election. A request to alter the amount of Compensation deferred shall be
submitted by Participant in writing to the Fiduciary Committee. The application shall set forth in detail the reasons for the requested reduction. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE&nbsp;IV<BR>
COMPANY CONTRIBUTIONS  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4.01</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Company Discretionary Contributions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;For each Plan Year, the Company may, in its discretion, make a
contribution to each Participant's Benefit Account in a dollar amount to be determined by Company. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4.02</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Company Matching Contributions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company may make, in its discretion, a matching contribution for each
Plan Year to each Participant's Benefit Account equal to the excess of (a)&nbsp;over (b)&nbsp;below: </FONT></P>

<UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A
percentage multiplied by the Participant's total Compensation for the Plan Year. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
total amount of matching contributions made on the Participant's behalf under the Company's Section&nbsp;401(k) Plan for the Plan Year. </FONT></P>

</UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>In
order to be eligible to receive a Company Matching Contribution under this Plan, the Participant must have elected to defer in the Section&nbsp;401(k) Plan the maximum deferral eligible to be
matched under the Section&nbsp;401(k) Plan. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE&nbsp;V<BR>
UNFUNDED STATUS AND LIFE INSURANCE  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5.01</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Unfunded Status.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;All benefits payable under this Plan shall be paid as they become due and payable by the
Company out of its general assets. In the event the Company, in its sole discretion, decides to fund all or any part of the benefits payable under this Plan with contributions to a separate fund, the
Company shall maintain separate accounts for each Participant to which such contributions are allocated. Nothing contained in this Plan shall be deemed to require a trust of any kind for the benefit
of the Participants or create any fiduciary relationship between the Company and the Participants or their Beneficiaries. To the extent that any person acquires a right to receive benefits under this
Plan, such rights shall be no greater than the right of any unsecured general creditor of the Company. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5.02</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Life Insurance.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company's obligation under this Plan shall be an unfunded and unsecured promise to pay.
The Company shall not be required to fund its obligations, but the Company, in its sole discretion, may apply for and own for its own benefit, insurance on the life of a Participant in such amounts
and in such forms as the Company may choose. The Participant shall have no interest whatsoever in any such policy or policies, but at the request of the Company shall submit to medical examinations
and shall accurately and truthfully supply such information and execute such documents as may be required by the insurance company or companies to whom the Company has applied for insurance. The
Company shall be under no obligation to provide the benefits in Article&nbsp;VII of this Plan if the Participant fails to comply with these provisions. Any insurance policy acquired by or held by
the Company in connection with the liabilities assumed by it pursuant to the Plan shall not be </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>4</FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=4,SEQ=4,EFW="2155658",CP="THE SPORTS AUTHORITY, INC.",DN="3",CHK=876686,FOLIO='4',FILE='DISK047:[05DEN0.05DEN1680]KM1680A.;8',USER='MBRADT',CD='14-APR-2005;15:32' -->
<A NAME="page_km1680_1_5"> </A>
<BR>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>deemed
to be held under any trust for the benefit of the Participant, the Participant's Beneficiary or estate, or to be security for the performance of the obligations of the Company but shall be, and
remain, a general, unpledged and unrestricted asset of the Company. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE&nbsp;VI<BR>
PARTICIPANT BENEFIT ACCOUNT AND VESTING  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6.01</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Benefit Account.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company shall establish a Benefit Account on its books for each Participant, and shall
credit to each Participant's Benefit Account the following amounts at the times specified: </FONT></P>

<UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Participant Disallowed 401(k) Contributions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> Disallowed 401(k) contributions will equal the amount of Compensation the
Participant elects to defer pursuant to Article&nbsp;III of the Plan, credited within an administratively reasonable period of time after the amounts refunded from the Company's
Section&nbsp;401(k) Plan, as an excess deferral, excess contribution and/or excess aggregate contribution are deposited in the designated Benefit Account. The Company shall deduct from Participant's
Compensation any amounts it, in its sole discretion, determines that it is required to withhold under any state or federal law for taxes or other charges. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Participant Deferral Contributions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> Deferral contributions will equal the amount of Compensation the Participant elects
to defer pursuant to Article&nbsp;III of the Plan, credited on the day the amounts are deposited in the designated Benefit Account. The Company shall deduct from Participant's Compensation any
amounts it, in its sole discretion, determines that it is required to withhold under any state or federal law for taxes or other charges. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Participant Bonus Contributions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> Bonus Contributions will equal the amount of bonus the Participant elects to defer
pursuant to Article&nbsp;III of the Plan, credited on the day the amounts are deposited in the designated Benefit Account. The Company shall deduct from Participant's Compensation any amounts it, in
its sole discretion, determines that it is required to withhold under any state or federal law for taxes or other charges. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Company Discretionary Contributions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> Company Discretionary Contributions will equal the amount of Company Discretionary
Contributions made pursuant to Article&nbsp;IV of the Plan, credited on the day the amounts are deposited in the designated Benefit Account. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(e)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Company Matching Contributions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> Company Matching Contributions will equal the amount of Company Matching Contributions
made pursuant to Article&nbsp;IV of the Plan, credited on the day the amounts are deposited in the designated Benefit Account. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(f)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Earnings and Losses.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> As of each valuation date, earnings and losses with respect to each Benefit Account will be
allocated, with respect to the investment options elected by Participant. </FONT></P>

</UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A
Participant's Benefit Account shall be utilized solely as a device for the measurement and determination of the amounts to be paid to the Participant pursuant to this Plan. A
Participant's Benefit Account shall not constitute or be treated as a trust fund of any kind. All benefits payable under this Plan shall be paid as they become due and payable by the Company out of
its general assets. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6.02</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Account Balance.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Participant's Account Balance as of each Determination Date shall consist of the
balance of the Participant's Benefit Account as of the immediately preceding Determination Date plus the amounts required to be credited to such account by the Company pursuant to Section&nbsp;6.01
and any applicable earnings, less the amount of all distributions, if any, made from such Benefit Account since the immediately preceding Determination Date, and any applicable losses. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>5</FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=5,SEQ=5,EFW="2155658",CP="THE SPORTS AUTHORITY, INC.",DN="3",CHK=157347,FOLIO='5',FILE='DISK047:[05DEN0.05DEN1680]KM1680A.;8',USER='MBRADT',CD='14-APR-2005;15:32' -->
<A NAME="page_km1680_1_6"> </A>
<BR>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6.03</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Statement Account.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Fiduciary Committee shall provide to each Participant quarterly an account statement
setting forth the balance to the credit of such Participant in his Benefit Account as of the last day of the preceding calendar quarter. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6.04</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Vesting of Benefit Account.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Contributions made to this Plan shall be vested as follows: </FONT></P>

<UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Participant Contributions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> Participant contributions to the Plan, meaning Participant Disallowed 401(k) Contributions,
Participant Deferral Contributions and Participant Bonus Contributions, including all earnings and losses thereon, shall be 100% vested at all times. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Company Discretionary and Matching Contributions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> If Termination of Employment with the Company occurs prior to attaining
Normal Retirement Age, the Participant's benefit shall be nonforfeitable under the same vesting rules as provided in the Section&nbsp;401(k) Plan sponsored in the Section&nbsp;401(k) Plan
sponsored by the Company. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding
the provisions of (b)&nbsp;above, a Participant's benefit under the Plan shall become 100% vested if any of the following events occur prior to the
Participant's Termination of Employment with the Company: (1)&nbsp;the Company experiences a Change of Control; or (2)&nbsp;the Participant attains Normal Retirement Age. </FONT></P>

</UL>
<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE&nbsp;VII<BR>
PAYMENT OF BENEFITS  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7.01</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Benefit Payments Prior to Termination of Employment.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Participants may elect to receive distribution of the
vested portion of their Benefit Account prior to Termination of Employment ("In-Service Distributions") on a form to be provided by the Fiduciary Committee. Amounts elected for
In-Service Distributions must (a)&nbsp;have remained in the Plan for at least one (l)&nbsp;Plan Year before distribution, measured from the beginning of the Plan Year in which such
contributions were allocated and (b)&nbsp;such election form must be received by the Fiduciary Committee prior to the beginning of the Plan Year to which such In-Service Distribution is
requested. Company Discretionary Contributions shall be distributed to the Participant after such contributions have remained in the Plan for at least one (1)&nbsp;year, measured from the beginning
of the initial Plan Year in which such contributions are allocated, unless the Participant elects to defer distribution of such contributions further in the manner specified herein. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7.02</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Benefit Payments Upon Termination of Employment.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Upon a Participant's termination of employment for any
reason, voluntary or involuntary, including by reason of retirement, Disability or death, the Participant (or the Participant's Beneficiaries, if applicable) shall receive a benefit equal to the
vested portion of the Participant's Benefit Account. The form, timing and term of the benefit shall be determined as follows: </FONT></P>

<UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Upon
a Participant's Involuntary Termination, the benefit shall be payable in a lump sum or installments for a period of not more than one year, as soon as
administratively practical after the Involuntary Termination; </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Upon
a Participant's Termination of Employment on account of (1)&nbsp;attainment of Early Retirement Age, (2)&nbsp;death, or (3)&nbsp;Disability, as soon as
administratively practical after termination of employment in accordance with the Participant's elections on forms required by the Fiduciary Committee; and </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Upon
a Participant's Termination of Employment for any reason other than those specified in Section&nbsp;7.02(a) or 7.02(b), as soon as administratively practical
after termination of employment in accordance with the Participant's elections on forms required by the Fiduciary Committee, provided, however, that the term of payment shall not exceed five years. </FONT></P>

</UL>
<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>6</FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=6,SEQ=6,EFW="2155658",CP="THE SPORTS AUTHORITY, INC.",DN="3",CHK=856650,FOLIO='6',FILE='DISK047:[05DEN0.05DEN1680]KM1680A.;8',USER='MBRADT',CD='14-APR-2005;15:32' -->
<A NAME="page_km1680_1_7"> </A>
<UL>
<BR>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Regardless
of (a), (b)&nbsp;or (c)&nbsp;above, if the Participant's Benefit Account is $10,000 or less, the benefit shall be paid in a lump sum as soon as
administratively practical after termination of employment. </FONT></P>

</UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7.03</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Survivor Benefit Before Termination of Employment.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If a Participant dies before commencement of benefits
while this Plan is in force and before Termination of Employment, the Participant's designated Beneficiary shall receive a benefit equal to the Participant's Benefit Account. The form and term of the
benefit shall be determined in accordance with the Participant's elections on forms provided by the Fiduciary Committee. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7.04</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Survivor Benefit After Termination of Employment.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If a Participant dies before commencement of benefits
while this Plan is in force and after Termination of Employment, the Participant's designated Beneficiary shall receive a benefit equal to the Participant's Benefit Account. The form and term of the
benefit shall be determined in accordance with the Participant's elections on forms provided by the Fiduciary Committee. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7.05</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Survivor Benefit After Commencement of Payments.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If a Participant dies while receiving benefits herein
described but before receiving the entire vested Benefit Account, the balance of the Benefit Account shall be paid to the Beneficiary in accordance with the Participant's elections. If the Beneficiary
dies before receiving the remaining vested Benefit Account, the remainder of the vested Benefit Account shall be paid to the estate of the Beneficiary. Payments to the estate of such Beneficiary may
be converted to lump sum if so elected by the Participant on forms provided by the Fiduciary Committee. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7.06</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Hardship Distribution.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Fiduciary Committee, under uniform and non-discriminatory rules,
upon finding that a terminated Participant has suffered a Hardship or is suffering a Hardship as defined in Section&nbsp;1.17, may distribute to such Participant all or a portion of the vested
Account Balance. The amount of any early distribution shall not exceed the amount required to meet such Hardship and is not reasonably available from other resources of the Participant. A
Participant's elections with respect to Bonus Contributions, Deferral Contributions and Disallowed 401(k) Contributions will be suspended for the remainder of the Plan Year upon a Hardship
distribution. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7.07</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Employment by a Successor Company.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the Participant terminates employment with the Company under a plan
of reorganization in which the Participant is employed by a Successor Company, the Participant will continue to participate in the Plan and will be eligible to receive a distribution upon a subsequent
termination of employment with the Successor Company. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7.08</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Recipients of Payments: Designation of Beneficiary.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;All payments to be made by the Company shall be made to
the Participant, if living. In the event of a Participant's death prior to the receipt of all benefit payments, all subsequent payments to be made under the Plan shall be to the Beneficiary or
Beneficiaries of the Participant. Each Participant shall file in writing with the Company a designation of Beneficiary and contingent Beneficiary to whom the Participant's interest under the Plan
shall be paid in the event of death. Such designation may be changed by the Participant at any time and without the consent of any previously designated Beneficiary. In the absence of an effective
Beneficiary designation as to any portion of a Participant's Benefit Account under the Plan or if the Beneficiary cannot be located, such amount shall be paid to the Participant's estate. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In
the event a benefit is payable to a minor or person declared incompetent or incapable of handling the disposition of his or her property, the Fiduciary Committee may pay such benefit
to the guardian, legal representative or person having the care or custody of such minor, incompetent or incapable person. The Fiduciary Committee may require proof of incompetency, minority
guardianship as it may deem appropriate prior to distribution of the benefit. Such distribution shall completely discharge the Company from all liability with respect to such benefit. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>7</FONT></P>

<P style='page-break-before:always'></p>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE&nbsp;VIII<BR>
ADMINISTRATION  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8.01</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Fiduciary Committee.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Plan shall be administered, interpreted and enforced by the Fiduciary Committee in
accordance with its terms and purposes. The Fiduciary Committee shall be appointed by an officer of the Company and shall consist of three (3)&nbsp;or more persons to act on behalf of the Company.
Interpretation by the Fiduciary Committee shall be final and binding upon a Participant except for the procedure set forth in Section&nbsp;8.03. No further appeal from a decision on review shall be
permitted. The Fiduciary Committee shall select the participating Key Employees and determine the assumptions to be used in computing benefits under the Plan. The Fiduciary Committee may adopt rules
and regulations relating to the Plan as it may deem necessary or advisable for the administration of the Plan. No member of the Committee may act, vote or otherwise influence a decision of the
Committee specifically relating to his or her own participation in the Plan. In the administration of this Plan, the Committee may, from time to time, employ agents and delegate to them such
administrative duties as it sees fit and may, from time to time, consult with counsel who may be counsel to the Participant. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8.02</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Committee Procedure.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;All determinations of the Committee shall be made by not less than a majority of its
members present at the meeting at which a quorum is present. The existence of a quorum will be determined in accordance with the Fiduciary Committee charter. Any action required or permitted to be
taken at a meeting of the Committee may be taken without a meeting, if a unanimous written consent which sets forth the action is signed by each member of the Committee and filed with the minutes of
proceedings of the Committee. Service on the Committee shall constitute services as a director of the Company so that members of the Committee may be entitled to indemnification as set forth in the
Company's bylaws and reimbursement for their services as members of the Committee. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8.03</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Claim Procedures.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<UL>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;All
claims shall be filed in writing by the Participant, his or her Beneficiary or the authorized representative of the claimant, by completing such procedures as the
Fiduciary Committee shall require. Such procedures shall be reasonable and may include the completion of forms and the submission of documents and additional information. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If
a claim is denied, notice of denial shall be furnished by the Fiduciary Committee to the claimant within ninety (90)&nbsp;days after the receipt of the claim by the
Fiduciary Committee, unless special circumstances require an extension of time for processing the claim, in which event notification of the extension shall be provided to the Participant or
Beneficiary and the extension shall not exceed ninety (90)&nbsp;days. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
Fiduciary Committee shall provide adequate notice, in writing, to any claimant whose claim has been denied, setting forth the specific reasons for such denial,
specific reference to pertinent Plan provisions, a description of any additional material or information necessary for the claimant to perfect his or her claim and an explanation of why such material
or information is necessary, all written in a manner calculated to be understood by the claimant. Such notice shall include appropriate information as to the steps to be taken if the claimant wishes
to submit his or her claim for further review. The claimant or the claimant's authorized representative must request such review within a reasonable period of time prescribed by the Fiduciary
Committee. In no event shall such period of time be less than sixty (60)&nbsp;days. A decision on review shall be made not later than sixty (60)&nbsp;days after the Company's receipt of the
request for review. If special circumstances require a further extension of time for processing, a decision shall be rendered not later than one hundred twenty (120)&nbsp;days following the
Company's receipt of the request for review. If such an extension of time for review is required, written notice of the extension shall be furnished to the claimant prior to the commencement of the
extension. The decision on review shall be furnished </FONT></P>

</UL>
<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>8</FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=8,SEQ=8,EFW="2155658",CP="THE SPORTS AUTHORITY, INC.",DN="3",CHK=339920,FOLIO='8',FILE='DISK047:[05DEN0.05DEN1680]KM1680A.;8',USER='MBRADT',CD='14-APR-2005;15:32' -->
<A NAME="page_km1680_1_9"> </A>
<UL>
<BR>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>to
the claimant. Such decision shall be in writing and shall include specific reasons for the decision, written in a manner calculated to be understood by the claimant, as well as specific references
to pertinent Plan provisions on which the decision is based. </FONT></P>

</UL>
<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2><B>ARTICLE&nbsp;IX<BR>
MISCELLANEOUS  </B></FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.01</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Employment Not Guaranteed by Plan.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Neither the Plan nor any action taken under the Plan shall be construed
as giving a Participant the right to be retained as a Key Employee or as an employee of the Company for any period. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.02</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Amendment and Termination.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company may, at any time, amend or terminate the Plan, provided that the
Company may not reduce or modify the vested portion of any Benefit Account prior to such amendment or termination. If the Company terminates the Plan, the Company shall distribute to the Participant
the amount of the Participant's vested Benefit Account. A Successor Company under a plan of reorganization may adopt the Plan for Participants employed by the Successor Company. With the approval of
the Board of Directors of the Company, all assets and liabilities may be transferred to the Successor Company for Participants employed by the Successor Company. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.03</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Merger/Direct Transfer.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Plan may enter into merger agreements or direct transfer of assets agreements
with the representatives of other deferred compensation or supplemental income plans, and accept the direct transfer of plan assets, or transfer plan assets, as a party to any such agreement. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.04</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Assignment of Benefits.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;No Participant or Beneficiary shall have the right to assign, transfer,
hypothecate, encumber or anticipate his or her interest in any benefits under this Plan, nor shall the benefits under this Plan be subject to any legal process to levy upon or attach the benefits for
payment of any claim against the Participant or his or her Beneficiary. Any attempted assignment or transfer by a Participant shall be null and void. In the event of any attempted assignment or
transfer, the Company shall have no further liability hereunder. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.05</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Disposition of Unclaimed Payments.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Participant must file with the Company from time to time, in
writing, his or her post office address and each change of post office address. The communication, statement or notice addressed to a Participant at the last post office address filed with the
Company, or if no address is filed with the Company, then at the last post office address as shown on the Company records, will be binding upon the Participant and his or her Beneficiaries for all
purposes of the Plan. If the Participant and his or her Beneficiaries cannot be located in this manner within 36&nbsp;months, the Fiduciary Committee will forfeit the Participant's Account. </FONT></P>


<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.06</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Taxes.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company shall deduct from all payments made hereunder all applicable federal or state taxes that
it, in its sole discretion, determines is required by law to be withheld from such payments. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.07</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Independence of Benefits.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The benefits payable under this Plan shall be independent of, and in addition to,
any other benefits or compensation whether by salary or bonus. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.08</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Governing Law.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This Plan is intended to constitute an unfunded Plan for a select group of management or
highly compensated employees and directors and rights thereunder shall be governed by the laws of the State of Colorado, except to the extent preempted by Federal law. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.09</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Form of Communication.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Any election, application, claim, notice or other communication required or
permitted to be made by a Participant to the Fiduciary Committee shall be made in writing and in such form as the Fiduciary Committee shall prescribe. Such communication shall be effective </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER"><FONT SIZE=2>9</FONT></P>

<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=9,SEQ=9,EFW="2155658",CP="THE SPORTS AUTHORITY, INC.",DN="3",CHK=1044108,FOLIO='9',FILE='DISK047:[05DEN0.05DEN1680]KM1680A.;8',USER='MBRADT',CD='14-APR-2005;15:32' -->
<A NAME="page_km1680_1_10"> </A>
<BR>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>upon
mailing, if sent by first class mail, postage pre-paid, and addressed to the Company's offices at: 1050 W. Hampden Avenue, Englewood, Colorado 80110. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.10</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Severability.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If any provision of this Plan is held to be illegal, invalid or unenforceable under present
or future laws, such provision shall be fully severable; this Plan shall be construed and enforced as if such illegal, invalid or unenforceable provision had never comprised a part of this Plan; and
the remaining provision of this Plan shall remain in full force and effect and shall not be affected by the illegal, invalid or unenforceable provision or by its severance from this Plan. Furthermore,
in lieu of
each such illegal, invalid or unenforceable provision, there shall be added automatically as part of this Plan a provision as similar in terms to such illegal, invalid or unenforceable provision as
may be possible and be legal, valid or enforceable. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.11</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Binding Agreement.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The provisions of this Plan shall be binding upon the Participants, and the Company and
their successors, assigns, heirs, executors and beneficiaries. </FONT></P>

<P><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ACCEPTED
by the Company on the&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;day of&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;. </FONT></P>
